NOTIFICATIONS  BY  GOVERNMENT
II-2--Ex-- (611)
[ 1 ]
WATER RESOURCES DEPARTMENT
ACQUISITION OF LANDS
FORM VI
(See Rule 16)
DECLARATION
[
No. II(2)/WR/925(b-1)/2021.
Whereas it appears to the Government that a total of 30.88.38 hectares of land is required in the 
Ittamozhi Village in Thisaiyanvilai Taluk in Tirunelveli District for public purpose namely in Interlinking 
of Tamirabarani – Karumeniyar – Nambiyar rivers for the Flood Carrier Canal Project.
Now, therefore a declaration is made hereby that a piece of land measuring 30.88.38 hectares is 
under acquisition for the above said project in the Ittamozhi Village in Thisaiyanvilai Taluk in Tirunelveli 
District whose detailed description is as follows:

30.88.38
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
This declaration is made after hearing of objections of persons interested and due enquiry as provided under section 15 of the Right to Fair Compensation 
and Transparency in Land Acquisition, Rehabilitation and Resettlement Act, 2013 (Central Act 30 of 2013). The number of families likely to be resettled due 
to land acquisition is Nil.
Mines of coal, iron-stone, slate or other minerals lying under the said land or any particular portion of the said land, except such parts of the mines 
and minerals which may be required to be dug or removed or used during the construction phase of the project for the purpose of which the land is being 
acquired, are not needed.
A plan of the land may be inspected in the oﬃ  ce of the Special Tahsildar, River Linking Project, Unit-2, Nanguneri and  Oﬃ  ce of the Executive Engineer, 
Water Resources Department, Special Project Division, Nanguneri and Public Works Department, Nambiyar Reservoir Project Division, Valliyoor on any working day.
 
 
SANDEEP  SAXENA,
 
 
Additional Cheif Secretary to Government.

DECLARATION
No.II(2)/WR/925(B-2)/2021.
Whereas it appears to the  Government that a total of 1.81.06 hectares of land is required in the Thiruvembalapuram Village in Radhapuram Taluk in 
Tirunelveli District for public purpose namely Interlinking of  Tamirabarani – Karumeniyar - Nambiyar rivers for the Flood Carrier Canal Project.
Now, therefore a declaration is made hereby that a piece of land measuring 1.81.06 hectares is under acquisition for the above said project in the 
Thiruvembalapuram Village in Radhapuram Taluk in Triunelveli District whose detailed description is as follows:

This declaration is made after hearing of objections of persons interested and due enquiry as provided under section 15 of the Right to Fair Compensation and Transparency in 
Land Acquisition, Rehabilitation and Resettlement Act, 2013 (Central Act 30 of 2013). The number of families likely to be resettled due to land acquisition is Nil.
Mines of coal, iron-stone, slate or other minerals lying under the said land or any particular portion of the said land, except such parts of the mines and minerals which 
may be required to be dug or removed or used during the construction phase of the project for the purpose of which the land is being acquired, are not needed.
A plan of the land may be inspected in the Oﬃ  ce of the  Special Tahsildar, River Linking Project, Unit-2, Nanguneri and  Oﬃ  ce of the  Executive Engineer, 
Water Resources Department, Special Project Division,  Ambasamudram  on any working day.
 
SANDEEP SAXENA,
 
Additional Chief Secretary to Government.

17.95.55
 
This declaration is made after hearing of objections of persons interested and due enquiry as provided under section 15 of the Right to Fair Compensation 
and Transparency in Land Acquisition, Rehabilitation and Resettlement Act, 2013 (Central Act 30 of 2013). The number of families likely to be resettled due 
to land acquisition is Nil.
Mines of coal, iron-stone, slate or other minerals lying under the said land or any particular portion of the said land, except such parts of the mines 
and minerals which may be required to be dug or removed or used during the construction phase of the project for the purpose of which the land is being 
acquired, are not needed.
A plan of the land may be inspected in the oﬃ  ce of the Land Acquisition Oﬃ  cer, O/o. The Special Tahsildhar, River Linking Project, Unit-6, Radhapuram 
@ Nanguneri and  O/o Executive Engineer, Water Resources Department, Special  Project Division, Tirunelveli on any working day.
 
SANDEEP SAXENA,
 
Additional Chief Secretary to Government.
